#### <a name="azbatch"></a><span data-ttu-id="e993c-178">Az.Batch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-178">Az.Batch</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="e993c-179">Renommage de `CoreQuota` sur `BatchAccountContext` en `DedicatedCoreQuota`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-179">Renamed `CoreQuota` on `BatchAccountContext` to `DedicatedCoreQuota`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e993c-180">Il existe également un nouveau `LowPriorityCoreQuota`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-180">There is also a new `LowPriorityCoreQuota`.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="e993c-181">Cela a un impact sur **Get-AzBatchAccount**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-181">This impacts **Get-AzBatchAccount**.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="e993c-182">Le paramètre `-ResourceFile` **New-AzBatchTask** prend à présent une collection d’objets `PSResourceFile`, qui peuvent être construits à l’aide de la nouvelle applet de commande **New-AzBatchResourceFile**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-182">**New-AzBatchTask** `-ResourceFile` parameter now takes a collection of `PSResourceFile` objects, which can be constructed using the new **New-AzBatchResourceFile** cmdlet.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="e993c-183">Nouvelle applet de commande **New-AzBatchResourceFile** pour aider à créer des objets `PSResourceFile`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-183">New **New-AzBatchResourceFile** cmdlet to help create `PSResourceFile` objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e993c-184">Ceux-ci peuvent être fournis à **New-AzBatchTask** sur le paramètre `-ResourceFile`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-184">These can be supplied to **New-AzBatchTask** on the `-ResourceFile` parameter.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="e993c-185">Cela prend en charge deux nouveaux types de fichiers de ressources, en plus de la procédure `HttpUrl` existante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-185">This supports two new kinds of resource file in addition to the existing `HttpUrl` way:</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="e993c-186">Les fichiers de ressources basés sur `AutoStorageContainerName` téléchargent l’intégralité d’un conteneur de stockage automatique dans le nœud Batch.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-186">`AutoStorageContainerName` based resource files download an entire auto-storage container to the Batch node.</span></span>
    - <span data-ttu-id="e993c-187">Les fichiers de ressources basés sur `StorageContainerUrl` téléchargent le conteneur spécifié dans l’URL dans le nœud Batch.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-187">`StorageContainerUrl` based resource files download the container specified in the URL to the Batch node.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="e993c-188">Suppression de la propriété `ApplicationPackages` de `PSApplication` retournée par **Get-AzBatchApplication**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-188">Removed `ApplicationPackages` property of `PSApplication` returned by **Get-AzBatchApplication**.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="e993c-189">Les packages spécifiques à l’intérieur d’une application peuvent maintenant être récupérés à l’aide de **Get-AzBatchApplicationPackage**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-189">The specific packages inside of an application now can be retrieved using **Get-AzBatchApplicationPackage**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e993c-190">Par exemple : `Get-AzBatchApplication -AccountName myaccount -ResourceGroupName myresourcegroup -ApplicationId myapplication`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-190">For example: `Get-AzBatchApplication -AccountName myaccount -ResourceGroupName myresourcegroup -ApplicationId myapplication`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="e993c-191">Renommage de `ApplicationId` en `ApplicationName` sur **Get-AzBatchApplicationPackage**, **New-AzBatchApplicationPackage**, **Remove-AzBatchApplicationPackage**, **Get-AzBatchApplication**, **New-AzBatchApplication**, **Remove-AzBatchApplication** et **Set-AzBatchApplication**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-191">Renamed `ApplicationId` to `ApplicationName` on **Get-AzBatchApplicationPackage**, **New-AzBatchApplicationPackage**, **Remove-AzBatchApplicationPackage**, **Get-AzBatchApplication**, **New-AzBatchApplication**, **Remove-AzBatchApplication**, and **Set-AzBatchApplication**.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="e993c-192">`ApplicationId` est maintenant un alias de `ApplicationName`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e993c-192">`ApplicationId` now is an alias of `ApplicationName`.</span></span>
